security\n"""\n\nimport jwt\nimport secrets\nimport hashlib\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom typing import Dict, Optional, Tuple\nimport logging\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\nclass AuthenticationSystem:\n    """JWT-based authentication system"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, secret_key: Optional[str] = None):\n        """\n        Initialize authentication system\n        \n        Args:\n            secret_key: Secret key for JWT signing (generates if not provided)\n        """\n        self.secret_key = secret_key or secrets.token_hex(32)\n        self.algorithm = \'HS256\'\n        self.token_expiry_hours = 24\n        \n        # In-memory user store (for demo - use database in production)\n        self.users = {\n            \'admin\': {\n                \'password_hash\': self._hash_password(\'admin123\'),\n                \'role\': \'admin\',\n                \'created_at\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n            },\n            \'demo\': {\n                \'password_hash\': self._hash_password(\'demo123\'),\n                \'role\': \'user\',\n                \'created_at\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n            }\n        }\n        \n        # Active tokens (for demo - use Redis in production)\n        self.active_tokens = set()\n        \n        logger.info("✓ Authentication System initialized")\n    \n    def _hash_password(self, password: str) -> str:\n        """Hash password using SHA-256"""\n        return hashlib.sha256(password.encode()).hexdigest()\n    \n    def verify_password(self, username: str, password: str) -> bool:\n        """Verify user password"""\n        user = self.users.get(username)\n        if not user:\n            return False\n        password_hash = self._hash_password(password)\n        return password_hash == user[\'password_hash\']\n    \n    def generate_token(self, username: str) -> str:\n        """\n        Generate JWT token for user\n        \n        Args:\n            username: Username to generate token for\n            \n        Returns:\n            JWT token string\n        """\n        if username not in self.users:\n            raise ValueError(f"User \'{username}\' not found")\n        \n        payload = {\n            \'username\': username,\n            \'role\': self.users[username][\'role\'],\n            \'iat\': datetime.utcnow(),\n            \'exp\': datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(hours=self.token_expiry_hours)\n        }\n        \n        token = jwt.encode(payload, self.secret_key, algorithm=self.algorithm)\n        self.active_tokens.add(token)\n        \n        logger.info(f"Token generated for user: {username}")\n        return token\n    \n    def verify_token(self, token: str) -> Tuple[bool, Optional[Dict]]:\n        """\n        Verify JWT token\n        \n        Args:\n            token: JWT token string\n            \n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (is_valid, payload_dict)\n        """\n        try:\n            # Check if token is active\n            if token not in self.active_tokens:\n                logger.warning("Token not found in active tokens")\n                return False, None\n            \n            # Decode token\n            payload = jwt.decode(\n                token,\n                self.secret_key,\n                algorithms=[self.algorithm]\n            )\n            \n            logger.info(f"Token verified for user: {payload.get(\'username\')}")\n            return True, payload\n            \n        except jwt.ExpiredSignatureError:\n            logger.warning("Token expired")\n            return False, None\n        except jwt.InvalidTokenError:\n            logger.warning("Invalid token")\n            return False, None\n    \n    def revoke_token(self, token: str) -> bool:\n        """\n        Revoke JWT token\n        \n        Args:\n            token: JWT token to revoke\n            \n        Returns:\n            True if revoked successfully\n        """\n        if token in self.active_tokens:\n            self.active_tokens.remove(token)\n            logger.info("Token revoked successfully")\n            return True\n        return False\n    \n    def logout(self, token: str) -> bool:\n        """Logout user by revoking token"""\n        return self.revoke_token(token)\n    \n    def add_user(self, username: str, password: str, role: str = \'user\') -> bool:\n        """\n        Add new user\n        \n        Args:\n            username: Username\n            password: Password (will be hashed)\n            role: User role (admin/user)\n            \n        Returns:\n Optional[str]:\n        """Get user role"""\n        user = self.users.get(username)\n        return user[\'role\'] if user else None\n    \n    def get_stats(self) -> Dict:\n        """Get {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="auth_middleware.py">\n"""\nMurphy System - Authentication Middleware\nFlask decorators for authentication and authorization\n"""\n\nfrom functools import wraps\nfrom flask import request, jsonify, g\nimport logging\nfrom typing import Callable, Optional\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\ndef require_auth(auth_system, roles: Optional[list] = None):\n    """\n    Decorator to require authentication for endpoints\n    \n    Args:\n        auth_system: AuthenticationSystem instance\n        roles: List of required roles (None = any authenticated user)\n    \n    Usage:\n        @app.route(\'/api/protected\')\n        @require_auth(auth_system)\n        def protected_endpoint():\n            return jsonify({\'user\': g.user})\n        \n        @app.route(\'/api/admin\')\n        @require_auth(auth_system, roles=[\'admin\'])\n        def admin_endpoint():\n            return jsonify({\'message\': \'Admin only\'})\n    """\n    def decorator(f: Callable) -> Callable:\n        @wraps(f)\n        def decorated_function(*args, **kwargs):\n            # Get token from Authorization header\n            auth_header = request.headers.get(\'Authorization\')\n            \n            if not auth_header:\n                logger.warning("Authentication required: No Authorization header")\n                return jsonify({\n                    \'success\': False,\n                    \'error\': \'authentication_required\',\n                    \'message\': \'Authentication required. Provide Bearer token in Authorization header.\'\n                }), 401\n            \n            # Extract token\n            if not auth_header.startswith(\'Bearer \'):\n                logger.warning("Authentication failed: Invalid token format")\n                return jsonify({\n                    \'success\': False,\n                    \'error\': \'invalid_token_format\',\n                    \'message\': \'Invalid token format. Use: Bearer <token>\'\n                }), 401\n            \n            token = auth_header[7:]  # Remove \'Bearer \' prefix\n            \n            # Verify token\n            is_valid, payload = auth_system.verify_token(token)\n            \n            if not is_valid or not payload:\n                logger.warning("Authentication failed: Invalid token")\n                return jsonify({\n                    \'success\': False,\n                    \'error\': \'invalid_token\',\n                    \'message\': \'Invalid or expired token\'\n                }), 401\n            \n            # Check role if specified\n            if roles:\n                user_role = payload.get(\'role\')\n                if user_role not in roles:\n                    logger.warning(f"Authorization failed: User role \'{user_role}\' not in {roles}")\n                    return jsonify({\n                        \'success\': False,\n                        \'error\': \'insufficient_permissions\',\n                        \'message\': f\'Insufficient permissions. Required roles: {", ".join(roles)}\'\n                    }), 403\n            \n            # Store user info in Flask\'s g object\n            g.user = {\n                \'username\': payload.get(\'username\'),\n                \'role\': payload.get(\'role\')\n            }\n            \n            logger.info(f"Authenticated: {g.user[\'username\']} (role: {g.user[\'role\']})")\n            \n            return f(*args, **kwargs)\n        \n        return decorated_function\n    return decorator\n\n\ndef optional_auth(auth_system):\n    """\n    Decorator for optional authentication\n    Attaches user info to g.user if authenticated, but doesn\'t require it\n    \n    Args:\n        auth_system: AuthenticationSystem instance\n    \n    Usage:\n        @app.route(\'/api/public\')\n        @optional_auth(auth_system)\n        def public_endpoint():\n            if hasattr(g, \'user\'):\n                return jsonify({\'user\': g.user})\n            return jsonify({\'message\': \'Anonymous\'})\n    """\n    def decorator(f: Callable) -> Callable:\n        @wraps(f)\n        def decorated_function(*args, **kwargs):\n            # Try to authenticate, but don\'t require it\n            auth_header = request.headers.get(\'Authorization\')\n            \n            if auth_header and auth_header.startswith(\'Bearer \'):\n                token = auth_header[7:]\n                is_valid, payload = auth_system.verify_token(token)\n                \n                if is_valid and payload:\n                    g.user = {\n                        \'username\': payload.get(\'username\'),\n                        \'role\': payload.get(\'role\')\n                    }\n            \n            return f(*args, **kwargs)\n        \n        return decorated_function\n    return decorator\n\n\ndef rate_limit(limit: int, per: int = 60):\n    """\n    Decorator for rate limiting (simple implementation)\n    \n    Args:\n        limit: Number of requests allowed\n        per: Time period in seconds\n    \n    Usage:\n        @app.route(\'/api/limited\')\n        @rate_limit(limit=10, per=60)\n        def limited_endpoint():\n            return jsonify({\'message\': \'Limited endpoint\'})\n    """\n    def decorator(f: Callable) -> Callable:\n        @wraps(f)\n        def decorated_function(*args, **kwargs):\n            # Simple in-memory rate limiting (use Redis in production)\n            if not hasattr(decorated_function, \'request_counts\'):\n                decorated_function.request_counts = {}\n            \n            ip = request.remote_addr\n            current_time = int(__import__(\'time\').time())\n            \n            # Clean old entries\n            decorated_function.request_counts = {\n                k: v for k, v in decorated_function.request_counts.items()\n                if current_time - v[\'first_request\'] < per\n            }\n            \n            # Check rate limit\n            if ip in decorated_function.request_counts:\n                count = decorated_function.request_counts[ip][\'count\']\n                if count >= limit:\n                    logger.warning(f"Rate limit exceeded for IP: {ip}")\n                    return jsonify({\n                        \'success\': False,\n                        \'error\': \'rate_limit_exceeded\',\n                        \'message\': f\'Rate limit exceeded.
